MEN'S AIR JORDAN 5 RETRO 'TOP 3'
mitmproxy

	Full-grain leather upper on the Air Jordan Retro 5
	Encapsulated Air-Sole units for responsive cushioning
	PU midsole for soft, plush cushioning
	Flex grooves help promote natural movement
	Herringbone outsole for traction
	The Air Jordan Retro 5 is imported


In 1990, Michael Jordans game was on the rise and few could match the way he attacked opponents on the court. As a nod to Jordan's on-court play, the Men's Air Jordan Retro 5 Basketball Shoes were designed to look like a fighter plane. In the famed model, MJ earned his fourth consecutive scoring title, sixth All-Star appearance and led the Bulls to the Eastern Conference Finals.

Two Things!

1. I love how slimming black makes me look and these nike Zoom 2k kicks will always be always be a favorite! I got these from finishline months ago, but they do still have them in stock if youre interested!

2. I cant wait until its safe to actually put on my outdoor clothes and hangout again! Although South Carolina is almost completely open again. Its no where near safe to be out right now. Now I dont watch the news or read the news articles (for my own peace of mind), but I just learned from my fam that there are 3,000 more cases in SC since last week. I made a quick run to the post office today and the amount of people I saw out at non-essential places was ridiculous! I honestly dont know what people are thinking right now. But I know what Jay will be doing okay.

What are they saying where you are? Are things opening back up?

Two Things!

1. I love how slimming black makes me look and these nike Zoom 2k kicks will always be always be a favorite! I got these from finishline months ago, but they do still have them in stock if youre interested!

2. I cant wait until its safe to actually put on my outdoor clothes and hangout again! Although South Carolina is almost completely open again. Its no where near safe to be out right now. Now I dont watch the news or read the news articles (for my own peace of mind), but I just learned from my fam that there are 3,000 more cases in SC since last week. I made a quick run to the post office today and the amount of people I saw out at non-essential places was ridiculous! I honestly dont know what people are thinking right now. But I know what Jay will be doing okay.
